                                 ARTICLE 45 - TERMINATION                                         <br /><br /><br />
45.1    The GOVERNMENT shall have the right, subject to the provisions of Article 45.5.           <br /><br /><br />
to terminate this Contract in the event the CONTRACTOR                                            <br /><br /><br />
(a)    fails to meet a material financial obligation expressly stated in this Conti act. or       <br /><br /><br />
(b)    during the First Sub-Period dees not cany out drilling ar.d seismic acquisition,           <br /><br /><br />
as detailed in Article 10.2 or. during the Second Sub-Period (or earlier), does                   <br /><br /><br />
not carry out drilling and seismic acquisition, as detailed in Article 10.3. or                   <br /><br /><br />
(c)    interrupts Production for a period of more than ninety (90) consecutive days               <br /><br /><br />
with no cause or justification acceptable in accordance with this Contract or                     <br /><br /><br />
under prudent international petroleum industry practice, it being recognised                      <br /><br /><br />
that Force Manure is an acceptable justification for such interruptions; or                       <br /><br /><br />
(d)    intentionally extracts or produces any mineral which is not covered by die                 <br /><br /><br />
object of this Contract, unless such extraction or production is expressly                        <br /><br /><br />
authorised or unavoidable as a result of operations earned out in accordance                      <br /><br /><br />
with prudent international petroleum industry practice;                                           <br /><br /><br />
(c) if the CONTRACTOR comprises solely one entity, is declared bankrupt ir.                       <br /><br /><br />
accordance with applicable I.aw; or                                                               <br /><br /><br />
(f) wilfully refuses to abide by negotiation, mediation, arbitration or expert                    <br /><br /><br />
decision under Article 42.                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
45.2    The GOVERNMENT may also terminate the Contract only in respect of one                     <br /><br /><br />
CONTRACTOR Entity if such entity is subject to a Change of Control for which the                  <br /><br /><br />
GOVERNMENT has not given its authorisation in accordance with Article 39.7.                       <br /><br /><br />
45.3    At any time prior to the Development Period, the CONTRACTOR shat: have the                <br /><br /><br />
right to terminate this Contract by surrendering the entire Coo tract Area in accordance          <br /><br /><br />
with the provisions of Article 7.                                                                 <br /><br /><br />

To classify expenditures, define further Petroleum Costs (in addition to those defined       <br /><br /><br />
.is such in the Articles of the Contract), and prescribe the manner in which the             <br /><br /><br />

the other provisions of the Contract, then the other provisions of the Contract shall        <br /><br /><br />
prevail.                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />

Petroleum Costs arc made. The purposes which shall qualify are                                   <br /><br /><br />
